🧔🏼 => 🧔🏼, afụ ọnụ, ajị ọnụ, onye, ọtanjele ahụ maka ọcha-ndịna etiti

🧔🏾 => 🧔🏾, afụ ọnụ, ajị ọnụ, onye, ọtanjele ahụ maka òji-ndịna etiti
🧔🏿 => 🧔🏿, afụ ọnụ, ajị ọnụ, onye, ọtanjele ahụ maka òji
🧔🏻‍♂ => 🧔🏻‍♂, afụ ọnụ, nwoke, nwoke afụ ọnụ, ọtanjele ahụ maka ọcha
🧔🏼‍♂ => 🧔🏼‍♂, afụ ọnụ, nwoke, nwoke afụ ọnụ, ọtanjele ahụ maka ọcha-ndịna etiti
🧔🏽‍♂ => 🧔🏽‍♂, afụ ọnụ, nwoke, nwoke afụ ọnụ, ọtanjele ahụ ndịna etiti
🧔🏾‍♂ => 🧔🏾‍♂, afụ ọnụ, nwoke, nwoke afụ ọnụ, ọtanjele ahụ maka òji-ndịna etiti
🧔🏿‍♂ => 🧔🏿‍♂, afụ ọnụ, nwoke, nwoke afụ ọnụ, ọtanjele ahụ maka òji
👱🏻‍♂ => 👱🏻‍♂, isi awọ, nwoke, nwoke nwere isi-awọ, ọtanjele ahụ maka ọcha
👱🏼‍♂ => 👱🏼‍♂, isi awọ, nwoke, nwoke nwere isi-awọ, ọtanjele ahụ maka ọcha-ndịna etiti
👱🏽‍♂ => 👱🏽‍♂, isi awọ, nwoke, nwoke nwere isi-awọ, ọtanjele ahụ ndịna etiti
👱🏾‍♂ => 👱🏾‍♂, isi awọ, nwoke, nwoke nwere isi-awọ, ọtanjele ahụ maka òji-ndịna etiti
👱🏿‍♂ => 👱🏿‍♂, isi awọ, nwoke, nwoke nwere isi-awọ, ọtanjele ahụ maka òji
👨🏻‍❤‍💋‍👨🏻 => 👨🏻‍❤‍💋‍👨🏻, di na nwunye, ezigbo m, ịhụnanya, mkpakọrịta nwoke na nwaanyị, mwah, ncheta, nọkọta ọnụ, nsusu ọnụ, nwa, nwoke, obi, onye, ọtanjele ahụ maka ọcha, ọyị, xoxo
